name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Deluxe Multi-level Suite
info:Stayed in May 2024

info:3 Reviews
rating:3.5
posted:Posted May 8, 2024
msg:The hotel is far from the core scenic spots, but there is a subway just outside, which is quite convenient. (The nearest subway station to the hotel does not have an elevator to go downstairs, which is not friendly to passengers with large luggage.) The hotel rooms are spacious, the hardware facilities are also good, and there are fruits and free drinks on the first day.
The hotel has obvious advantages and many disadvantages. The biggest bug is that the curtains in the shower room are transparent. When taking a shower inside, you can clearly enjoy the silhouette outside; second, the room service is average, especially the waiter on duty on the night of May 3. I called the room service number and greeted "Hello!" after the call was connected. The waiter actually replied "Yeah!" I thought I heard it wrong, and said "Hello!" again, and he replied "Yeah!" This kind of service attitude is really the first time I have experienced it in a high-end hotel, let alone a guesthouse. The reason why the service is still given 3 points is that the waiter I met on the day of check-out was quite enthusiastic. Seeing that we were in a hurry, he took the initiative to ask us if we still needed water.
Another thing is that the washbasin operation table in the hotel is too small. The countertop will get wet after washing your face, and there is no place to put the toiletries bag. The hair dryer is also low, and it gets hot after blowing for a while.
